SRID NYI ZLA'I BGROD PA MA RDZOGS PAR, ,DE SRID RI DBANG LTA BUR
G-YO MED SHOG ,'JAM

DPAL SNYING PO'I CHOS SRID DE 'DZIN RNAMS, ,YUN RING BRTEN CING
PHYOGS BCUR 'PHEL BA DANG, ,MAR GYUR 'GRO RNAMS CHOS 'BYOR LONGS
SPYOD RGYAS, ,NYIN MTSAN RTAG TU DGE BA'I BKRA SHIS SHOG ,CES
RJE BTZUN BLO

BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN DPAL BZANG PO'I SPYOD TSUL GYI 'PHRO
KHRIGS SU BSGRIGS PA 'DI YANG, DANG LDAN MANG POS YANG YANG
BSKUL BA'I BLO NGO DANG BSTUN NAS, PHYAG MDZOD BLO BZANG DGE
LEGS DANG, MDZOD 'DZIN

PHUN TSOGS RAB BRTAN, GSOL DPON BLO BZANG BSTAN 'DZIN RNAMS KYIS
RJE DE NYID KYI GSUNG DANG MDZAD PA THUN MONG BA 'GA' ZHIG ZIN
BRIS SU BTAB 'DUG PA DANG, DGONGS PA YONGS SU RDZOGS PA'I CHED
DU SKU GSUNG THUGS RTEN

BZHENGS MCHOD 'GYIS PA, RIS MED KYI TSANGS SPYOD LDAN PA'I DGE
BDUN MANG PO LA RNYED BKUR BSGRUBS PA'I BRJED BYANG BKOD PA
RNAMS LA GZHI BYAS, SGRO SKUR GYI BRJOD BYA SPANGS TE, SH'AKYA'I
BTZUN PA BLO BZANG YE SHES

@225B KYIS KUN LDAN ZHES PA LCAGS PHO BYI BA'I LO STON ZLA THA
CHUNG GI LHA BABS DUS CHEN NYIN MJUG GRUB PAR SBYAR BA DGE LEGS
'PHEL, ,PA RI PRi TZTSA, ,SARBA MANGGA LAm, ,SVA STI, PHAN BDE'I
'BYUNG GNAS RGYAL BSTAN

YONGS 'DU'I LJON, ,RAB RGYAS 'GRO KUN THAR MCHOG 'BRAS BZANG LA,
,SPYOD PHYIR BKRA SHIS LHUN GRUB CHOS GRVA CHER, ,CHOS SBYIN
'DZAD MED DAL 'GRO'I RGYUN 'DI SPEL,, ,,SARBA DZA GA TAm,,
